#### Heritage Preservation
Safeguarding the sounds of yesterday
By carefully repairing aging and damaged media and converting analog formats to high-quality digital files, Iron Mountain is helping artists, estates, and labels safeguard musical legacies that would otherwise be lost to time.
[Learn more](https://www.ironmountain.com/resources/landing-pages/h/heritage-preservation)

### IT asset lifecycle management
We’re here to protect your data, drive IT efficiencies, and maximize the return on your IT hardware investment. As the number one provider of ITAD in North America, we offer end-to-end services, from deployment to disposition. Explore how we unlock value with a focus on IT reuse.
**Featured services and solutions:**
[Asset lifecycle management (ALM)](https://www.ironmountain.com/services/it-asset-lifecycle-management)|[Data center decommissioning](https://www.ironmountain.com/services/it-asset-lifecycle-management/data-center-decommissioning)|[IT asset disposition (ITAD) ](https://www.ironmountain.com/services/it-asset-lifecycle-management/secure-it-asset-disposition)|[Hardware Asset Management](https://www.ironmountain.com/services/it-asset-lifecycle-management/hardware-asset-management)

## Trusted global data center colocation provider
Iron Mountain Data Centers delivers industry-leading hyperscale and colocation data centers as one of the most trusted data center companies in the world. We help complex organizations unlock what’s possible with data centers that protect, connect, and activate data like never before. Our global 1.3GW portfolio spanning three continents empowers customers, including leading cloud and AI providers, to scale their data footprint and unlock greater value at every stage. We lead the data center industry in highly regulated compliance, environmental sustainability, physical security, and business continuity. As an experienced colocation provider and data center developer, we collaborate with our customers to build and support their long-term digital needs.
[About Us](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/about)
## Why choose Iron Mountain Data Centers?
![globe](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/images/brand/icons/transparent-background/globe.svg?h=72&iar=0&w=72&sc_lang=en)
### Scale & development expertise
Our data centers feature a range of [hyperscale](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/colocation/our-data-centers#hyperscale-data-centers)-ready campus facilities with power agreements in place that provide ample room for growth. As a trusted data center developer, we provide everything from a few racks to a turn-key global architecture or a full facility build, with the capacity and flexibility to accommodate your evolving needs. 
![speed](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/images/brand/icons/transparent-background/speed.svg?h=72&iar=0&w=72&sc_lang=en)
###  Speed to market 
Iron Mountain Data Centers meets the demands of enterprises, cloud and AI providers with [data center infrastructure](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/colocation/our-data-centers) built where you need to be, at speed and scale. Our experienced data center developers deliver turn-key facilities and campus-scale deployments for [hyperscale](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/colocation/our-data-centers#hyperscale-data-centers) customers, while our pre-built modular data centers are designed for enterprises looking for rapid activation.
![legal 1](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/images/brand/icons/transparent-background/legal-1.svg?h=72&iar=0&w=72&sc_lang=en)
###  Financial strength 
As part of Iron Mountain, a global leader in secure data management since 1951 and trusted by 95% of Fortune 1000 companies, we offer the financial stability and proven expertise you need in a [long-term data center partner](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/about) to protect, connect, and activate your critical business data.
![password security](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/images/brand/icons/transparent-background/password-security.svg?h=72&iar=0&w=72&sc_lang=en)
### Security & compliance
We are trusted by the world’s most heavily regulated companies and offer the highest available standards in physical and data [security](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/security-and-compliance#security). Our comprehensive [compliance](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/security-and-compliance#compliance) support is tailored to your industry, with multiple layers of physical security at all facilities, including ultra-secure [underground data centers](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/colocation/our-data-centers#underground-data-centers) ideal for backup and disaster recovery.
![clean global](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/images/brand/icons/transparent-background/clean-global.svg?h=72&iar=0&w=72&sc_lang=en)
###  Sustainability 
Award-winning new builds designed to BREAAM specs that minimize environmental impact, matched by 100% renewable energy and industry-leading 24/7 carbon-free energy (CFE) commitment. As the only multi-tenant data center provider with this comprehensive [sustainable](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/sustainability) commitment, our dedication to clean energy & green practices has established us as an industry leader in environmental stewardship.
. 
![corporate response 1](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/images/brand/icons/transparent-background/corpresponse-1.svg?h=72&iar=0&w=72&sc_lang=en)
###  Customer satisfaction 
Our excellent [Net Promoter Score](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/colocation/customer-solutions) demonstrates our commitment to customer service excellence. From simple cross-connects to full installs & data center builds. Our Service Level Agreements guarantee prompt, high-quality service with 24x7x365 support teams dedicated to your success.

## AI-ready data centers
Power your artificial intelligence and machine learning workloads with Iron Mountain's purpose-built AI-ready infrastructure. Our data centers provide the high-density power, advanced cooling systems including liquid cooling, and ultra-low latency connectivity that AI applications demand. From GPU clusters, AI inferencing deployments to large language models, our facilities are engineered to support the most demanding computational workloads while maintaining the security, compliance, and reliability standards that make us the trusted choice for AI innovators worldwide.

## Frequently asked questions
What is a data center?
A data center is a specialized facility that houses computer systems, servers, storage, and networking equipment in a controlled environment optimized for performance and reliability. Data centers provide the necessary power, cooling, physical security, and connectivity infrastructure to keep digital operations running 24x7x365. Modern data centers range from small server rooms to massive hyperscale facilities spanning hundreds of thousands of square feet.
What's the difference between hyperscale and retail colocation?
Retail colocation involves smaller deployments, such as renting individual racks or cages in a shared facility, while hyperscale data centers involve larger deployments, including the leasing of entire data halls and buildings with megawatts of custom infrastructure. Retail colocation is like renting an apartment; hyperscale is like building or leasing a custom warehouse.
What makes a data center AI-ready?
AI-ready data centers are specifically designed to handle the intensive computational requirements of artificial intelligence and machine learning workloads. Key features include high-density power infrastructure capable of supporting power-hungry GPU clusters and AI processors, advanced cooling systems that utilize liquid cooling to manage the significant heat generated by AI hardware, ultra-low latency network connectivity for real-time AI applications, and a flexible infrastructure that can quickly scale to accommodate rapidly evolving AI technologies. AI-ready facilities also maintain the same stringent security and compliance standards required for sensitive AI model training and deployment.
Why should companies leverage a data center instead of staying on-premises?
Using a professional data center offers numerous advantages over on-premises deployments, including: enhanced physical security with 24x7 monitoring; reliable power infrastructure with backup systems; professional cooling systems optimized for IT equipment; access to multiple network carriers for redundant connectivity; compliance with industry standards and regulations; scalability to grow as business needs change; and reduced capital expenditure by leveraging shared infrastructure rather than building your own facility.
What is a hyperscale data center?
Hyperscale data centers are massive facilities designed to efficiently support extensive cloud computing and big data storage needs. These facilities span between 100,000 to over 1,000,000 square feet and consume 20 to 150+ megawatts of power. They house between 100,000 to 500,000+ servers while maximizing space efficiency through high-density configurations, with individual racks drawing 10-150 kW or more of power. Hyperscale data centers are built to accommodate the massive infrastructure requirements of major cloud providers, internet companies, and large enterprises that need to deploy thousands of servers at scale with maximum efficiency and reliability.
How should I choose a data center? 
When selecting a data center provider, consider: geographic location and proximity to your business operations; physical security measures and compliance certifications; power capacity, redundancy, and reliability (including backup systems); cooling infrastructure and efficiency; available connectivity options and carrier diversity; scalability to accommodate future growth; sustainability practices and renewable energy usage; technical support availability and expertise; and the provider's financial stability and track record of reliability.

We are one of the world’s fastest-growing global colocation providers, extending and expanding our data center footprint into new markets as demand arises. Our data center platform includes 30+ data centers throughout 3 continents that enable and support the colocation, interconnection and services our customers need.
## Asia-Pacific data center locations
The Asia Pacific region is expected to account for half of the global colocation market by 2025. Our data center locations in Singapore and India give customers strategic regional reach and rich interconnection ecosystems, all with the uncompromising Iron Mountain approach to standards and services. Singapore straddles the sea cables connecting India, South East Asia, China, Japan and Australasia, while our facilities, and recent expansions in Delhi-NCR, Mumbai, Pune, Hyderabad, Bengaluru and Chennai offer significant capacity with unparalleled reach across India, the world’s second-largest telecommunications market. We are committed to a high standard of service and customer care and are pleased to support our customers throughout the APAC region.

## Europe, Middle East & Africa data center locations
The EMEA region continues to see strong demand and rapid data center growth, especially in the core FLAP (Frankfurt, London, Amsterdam, Paris) markets and emerging markets such as Madrid, Dublin and more. In response to that demand, we have been expanding our EMEA footprint, with major data center construction builds in Frankfurt, Amsterdam and London, Europe’s three leading colocation markets as well as in Madrid, one of Europe’s emerging markets. We have capacity throughout our EMEA data center footprint to meet the needs of our single cabinet customers to our most demanding hyperscale clients. Backed by robust connectivity options, high-touch customer support and industry leading sustainability and compliance certifications, we are well positioned to meet our EMEA customers needs.

## North America data center locations
Our North American data center footprint consists of data centers in 11 strategic markets. Our footprint includes enterprise, edge and hyperscale data centers in: Boston, Chicago, Denver, Kansas City, Miami, New Jersey, Ohio, Northern Virginia, Pennsylvania, Phoenix, Richmond and Scottsdale. Our facilities are certified by one of the industry’s most comprehensive compliance standards (Global ISO 50001, ISO 140001, FISMA High, FedRAMP and others) making our data centers ideal for regulated markets. As industry leaders in sustainability commitments, including [The Climate Pledge](https://www.theclimatepledge.com/) and the United Nations [24/7 Carbon-Free Energy (CFE) Compact](https://gocarbonfree247.com/), we are uniquely positioned to partner with customers who have sustainable and green goals.

Web Werks is now Iron Mountain Data Centers, bringing our global portfolio to Bangalore, India with BLR-1.

## Why choose our Bangalore data center (BLR-1)?
Located in the fast growing “Silicon Valley of India”, our Bangalore data center is an 80,000 ft2 facility, with 4 MW of IT capacity, situated in the Pattandur Agrahara region near a myriad of regional and global technology providers.
  1. 1.9-acre site
  2. 80,000 ft2 of space
  3. 4 MW capacity


  

**BLR-1:**[564, Pattandura Agrahara Main Road Whitefield Bengaluru -66, KAR -560048](https://www.google.com/maps/place/HCL+Technologies/@12.9848893,77.7405312,17z/data=!3m1!4b1!4m5!3m4!1s0x3bae11fd2f55b98b:0xa08baa177713fff!8m2!3d12.9848594!4d77.7427124)

## Our Bengaluru (Bangalore), India data center & colocation services
##### We provide a full range of certified monitoring, migration and engineering services at all of our facilities worldwide. If you need detailed NOC reporting, a user-friendly customer portal, or full-scale builds and migrations, we can provide a one-off, ongoing or global solution.
  

### Compliance
Trusted by some of the world’s most highly-regulated organizations, Iron Mountain is an industry leader in compliance. Reduce data center risk with our comprehensive compliance support including HIPAA, FISMA High, PCI-DSS, ISO 27001, and SOC 2/3.
### Security
We are the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. Both aboveground and underground, our highly secure data centers have enhanced physical and digital security layers.
### Smart Hands
At every Iron Mountain data center, we offer a full portfolio of remote smart hands services, covering rack and stack services, builds and installs, hardware, power and connectivity as well as general hands-on maintenance tasks. 
### NOC and Portal
Our Global Network Operations Center (GNOC) is your central point for customer communication and advocacy. Leverage our data center portal for ticketing, power & cooling audits, access logs, bandwidth reports and more.
### Network Connectivity
With Iron Mountain’s carrier-neutral networking and data center interconnect services, we’ll get you where you need to be. We offer a wide range of services including cross connects, virtual cross connects, direct internet access, metro waves, peering and internet exchanges as well as Cloud On-Ramp.
### Sustainability
We are firm in our commitment to renewable energy and sustainable data centers. Our facilities are matched by 100% renewable energy, and our customers can take credit for the green energy that Iron Mountain buys on their own sustainability reporting with Green Power Pass.
## Iron Mountain's BLR data center
### Proven track record
Iron Mountain is the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. The world’s most heavily regulated organizations have trusted us with their data for decades.
###  Global efficiency 
Energize your digital transformation at our Bangalore data centers via our cloud, network and IT service ecosystems. Enjoy remote data center management, unbeatable operational efficiency and seamless global scale and standards.
###  Hyperscale-ready 
Iron Mountain Data Centers facilities have been designed to scale to accommodate exacting, wholesale requirements of hyperscale cloud providers, government organizations, and global enterprises.
###  Grow as you go 
Rather than relying on legacy infrastructure, your business can deploy data center capacity just like the cloud - as and when you need it. At our Bangalore colocation facilities, choose from cabinets, cages, suites, and MODs, and adapt and scale as you go.
> ### Greenhost customer success story
> #### The challenge
> As a frontrunner in the web hosting industry, Greenhost needed a long-term colocation partner with a focus on sustainability. In 2007, when the search began, those partners were minimal. The company also needed to find a partner that was carrier-neutral and had strong security policies.
> #### The results
> Greenhost partnered with Iron Mountain, who has a shared focus on renewable energy and sustainability. The partnership has allowed Greenhost to become more efficient and innovative while leveraging an industry-leading security and compliance portfolio. The relationship has continued to grow for more than a decade.
> #### In their words
> _“Iron Mountain knows our business and we wouldn’t think of leaving. We are proud to work with Iron Mountain and we think that works both ways.”_
Founder & CEO, Greenhost

# Boston data center
Iron Mountain’s original greenfield data center provides a safe, scalable location west of downtown Boston with plenty of room for growth.

## Why choose our Boston data center (BOS-1)?
Iron Mountain BOS-1 is a 21,000 ft2 facility with 3.6 MW of power and significant potential to scale up on our 58-acre campus. Rated to withstand Category 4 hurricane winds.
  1. 58-acre site
  2. 21,000 ft2 of space
  3. 3.6 MW capacity


  

**BOS-1:**[171 Bearfoot Rd Northborough, MA 01532](https://www.google.com/maps/place/Iron+Mountain+Data+Centers+BOS-1/@42.3404792,-71.64007,17z/data=!4m15!1m8!3m7!1s0x89e3f44bd9e21557:0x55722f1727e7eab4!2s171+Bearfoot+Rd,+Northborough,+MA+01532,+USA!3b1!8m2!3d42.3404137!4d-71.6398017!16s%2Fg%2F11dxsmz18s!3m5!1s0x89e3f57cacdd3b47:0x36a075cdc908cc8d!8m2!3d42.3406218!4d-71.6398111!16s%2Fg%2F11j8vlxk93?entry=ttu)
[Contact Us](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/contact-us)
## Boston data center photo tour
![video thubmnail](https://img.youtube.com/vi/63Vu7-PGonQ/maxresdefault.jpg)
![Data Center Boston Cages](https://www.ironmountain.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fedge.sitecorecloud.io%2Fironmountain-c8dd68e9%2Fmedia%2Fproject%2Firon-mountain%2Firon-mountain%2Fimages%2Fservices-and-industries%2Fimdc%2Fhero-and-background-over-800px%2Fbos-1-data-center-cages.jpg%3Fh%3D480%26iar%3D0%26w%3D856%26sc_lang%3Den&w=1920&q=80)
Boston data center cages: Data center cages provide an additional layer of physical security in the form of metal fencing and customizable features.

## Boston data center overview
### At a glance
  * Quiet suburban location with room to grow
  * Award-winning design
  * Diverse NSP selection
  * Easy cloud and carrier access
  * Matched by 100% renewable power
  * Rated to withstand Category 4 hurricane winds


### Campus
  * 58-acre site
  * Boston suburb in Worcester County
  * 3.6 MW
  * 21,000 ft2 of usable floorspace
  * LEED Gold design with waterless cooling 
  * Highly efficient operation
  * Concurrently maintainable facility


### Ecosystems
  * 4 carriers on-site
  * Metro access to AWS, Azure
  * WAN connectivity options


### Compliance
  * NIST 800-53
  * FISMA HIGH
  * FedRAMP
  * CMMC
  * SOC 2 Type II, SOC 3
  * PCI-DSS
  * HIPAA
  * HITRUST
  * LEED Gold
  * ISO 9001, 27001, 50001, 14001, 22301
  * EPA Energy Star

## Our Boston, Massachusetts data center & colocation services
##### We provide a full range of certified monitoring, migration and engineering services at all of our facilities worldwide. If you need detailed NOC reporting, a user-friendly customer portal, or full-scale builds and migrations, we can provide a one-off, ongoing or global solution.
  

### Compliance
Trusted by some of the world’s most highly-regulated organizations, Iron Mountain is an industry leader in compliance. Reduce data center risk with our comprehensive compliance support including HIPAA, FISMA High, PCI-DSS, ISO 27001, and SOC 2/3.
### Security
We are the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. Both aboveground and underground, our highly secure data centers have enhanced physical and digital security layers.
### Smart Hands
At every Iron Mountain data center, we offer a full portfolio of remote smart hands services, covering rack and stack services, builds and installs, hardware, power and connectivity as well as general hands-on maintenance tasks. 
### NOC and Portal
Our Global Network Operations Center (GNOC) is your central point for customer communication and advocacy. Leverage our data center portal for ticketing, power & cooling audits, access logs, bandwidth reports and more.
### Network Connectivity
With Iron Mountain’s carrier-neutral networking and data center interconnect services, we’ll get you where you need to be. We offer a wide range of services including cross connects, virtual cross connects, direct internet access, metro waves, peering and internet exchanges as well as Cloud On-Ramp.
### Sustainability
We are firm in our commitment to renewable energy and sustainable data centers. Our facilities are matched by 100% renewable energy, and our customers can take credit for the green energy that Iron Mountain buys on their own sustainability reporting with Green Power Pass.
## Iron Mountain's BOS data center
### Proven track record
Iron Mountain is the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. The world’s most heavily regulated organizations have trusted us with their data for decades.
### Global efficiency 
Energize your digital transformation at our Virginia data centers via our cloud, network and IT service ecosystems. Enjoy remote data center management, unbeatable operational efficiency and seamless global scale and standards.
### Hyperscale-ready 
Iron Mountain Data Centers facilities have been designed to scale to accommodate exacting, wholesale requirements of hyperscale cloud providers, government organizations, and global enterprises.
###  Grow as you go 
Rather than relying on legacy infrastructure, your business can deploy data center capacity just like the cloud - as and when you need it. At our Virginia colocation facilities, choose from cabinets, cages, suites, and MODs, and adapt and scale as you go.
> ### Fender customer success story
> #### The challenge
> Fender needed a home for their mission-critical financial planning and e-commerce systems. They looked to maximize redundancy while reducing data center total cost of ownership. Also, Fender needed access to numerous services providers to support their evolving hybrid IT architecture.
> #### The results
> Fender has enjoyed 100% uptime to date and flexible terms that significantly reduced data center costs. They cited Iron Mountain’s certified engineers as the added bonus, relying on Iron Mountain data center services for on-demand needs, extending capabilities and staying focused on high value activities.
> #### In their words
> _“It's one thing to outsource your servers. It’s another to outsource the support for those servers—that’s what gives CIOs heartburn. Iron Mountain’s remote support has been spectacular. Not only do they respond quickly, but they have a team that is well-trained and professional and that gives us confidence that the job will be done right.”_
SVP for Global IT, CIO of Fender

# Chennai data centers
Our Chennai data center campus, located in Ambattur area, will provide 42 MW of power, with the first 23 MW expected at CHN-1 in 2026.

## Why choose our Chennai data centers (CHN-1 & CHN-2)?
Situated on a highly secure 4.3 acre site, our Chennai data center campus is located in the Ambattur area, in easy reach of the city center and about an hour from Chennai International Airport. With a phased roll-out targeting 2026 for CHN-1 and 2028 for CHN-2, the campus will offer customers a total of 42 MW of power. Two data centers with 8 data halls each will provide nearly 800,000 ft2 of AI-ready space, with on-site access to Tier 1 carriers and other connectivity and service providers.
  1. 4.3 acre secure site
  2. 23.2 MW at CHN-1, 19 MW at CHN-2
  3. 800,000 ft2 planned campus-wide


  

**CHN-1:** Plot No 83, MTH Road, Ambattur Industrial Estate, Ambattur, Chennai – 600 053 | **CHN-2:** Plot No 84, MTH Road, Ambattur Industrial Estate, Ambattur, Chennai – 600 053
[Contact Us](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/contact-us)
  * _On-site Access_
To all Tier 1 carriers
  * _One of India's_
Largest exporting hubs in Chennai
  * _2026-2028_
Phased completion for campus
  * _AI-ready_
IT infrastructure at scale

## Chennai data centers overview
### At a glance
  * 23.2 MW & 383,540 ft2 at CHN-1
  * 19 MW & 396,075 ft2 at CHN-2
  * 16 Data halls
  * CHN-1 target live date: 2026
  * CHN-2 target live date: 2028
  * Block N+2C redundancy
  * A/B underground feeds


### Campus
  * Ambattur, Chennai
  * 4.3 acre secure site
  * 2 data centers
  * 779,616 ft2 total space
  * 42 MW+
  * Onsite 230 kVA GI substation


### Ecosystems
  * Carrier-neutral, with all Tier 1 carriers on-site
  * Cloud neutral
  * Metro Wave connectivity
  * Dark Fiber
  * Redundant MMRs
  * Diverse fiber PoEs


### Compliance
  * TIA 942 Rated 3
  * Liquid Cooling compliant
  * IGBC Green Data Center (in process)
  * SOC 1, SOC 2
  * PCI-DSS
  * ISO 9001, 14001, 22301, 27001, 50001, 14064
  * [EC (Environmental Clearance) Standards](https://www.ironmountain.com/utility/legal/ec-standards)

## Our Chennai, India data center & colocation services
##### We provide a full range of certified monitoring, migration and engineering services at all of our facilities worldwide. If you need detailed NOC reporting, a user-friendly customer portal, or full-scale builds and migrations, we can provide a one-off, ongoing or global solution.
  

### Compliance
Trusted by some of the world’s most highly-regulated organizations, Iron Mountain is an industry leader in compliance. Reduce data center risk with our comprehensive compliance support including HIPAA, FISMA High, PCI-DSS, ISO 27001, and SOC 2/3.
### Security
We are the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. Both aboveground and underground, our highly secure data centers have enhanced physical and digital security layers.
### Smart Hands
At every Iron Mountain data center, we offer a full portfolio of remote smart hands services, covering rack and stack services, builds and installs, hardware, power and connectivity as well as general hands-on maintenance tasks. 
### NOC and Portal
Our Global Network Operations Center (GNOC) is your central point for customer communication and advocacy. Leverage our data center portal for ticketing, power & cooling audits, access logs, bandwidth reports and more.
### Network Connectivity
With Iron Mountain’s carrier-neutral networking and data center interconnect services, we’ll get you where you need to be. We offer a wide range of services including cross connects, virtual cross connects, direct internet access, metro waves, peering and internet exchanges as well as Cloud On-Ramp.
### Sustainability
We are firm in our commitment to renewable energy and sustainable data centers. Our facilities are matched by 100% renewable energy, and our customers can take credit for the green energy that Iron Mountain buys on their own sustainability reporting with Green Power Pass.
## Iron Mountain's CHN data centers
### Proven track record
Iron Mountain is the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. The world’s most heavily regulated organizations have trusted us with their data for decades.
### Global efficiency 
Energize your digital transformation at our Chennai data centers via our cloud, network and IT service ecosystems. Enjoy remote data center management, unbeatable operational efficiency and seamless global scale and standards.
### Hyperscale-ready 
Iron Mountain Data Centers facilities have been designed to scale to accommodate exacting, wholesale requirements of hyperscale cloud providers, government organizations, and global enterprises.
###  Grow as you go 
Rather than relying on legacy infrastructure, your business can deploy data center capacity just like the cloud - as and when you need it. At our Chennai colocation facilities, choose from cabinets, cages, and suites, and adapt and scale as you go.
> #### With Iron Mountain, we have a highly available, redundant computing environment for the cloud … that helps us meet customer demand today and allows us to expand quickly to support business growth tomorrow

# Chicago data center
Iron Mountain is planning a 315,000 Sq. Ft. 36 MW Chicago data center (CHI-1) in the suburb of Des Plaines near O'Hare International.
[Get a Quote](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/get-a-quote)

## Why choose our Chicago data center (CHI-1)?
Located in the Chicago suburb of Des Plaines, Illinois, our Chicago data center will offer a mix of retail colocation and hyperscale data center solutions all in the fifth largest data center market in the U.S. At full build, CHI-1 will offer 36 MW of IT capacity, with the first 8 MW expected to come online in 2025.
  1. 13-acre site
  2. 315,000 ft2of space
  3. 36 MW total capacity


  

**CHI-1:** [1680 Touhy Avenue Des Plaines, IL 60018](https://www.google.com/maps/place/Iron+Mountain/@42.0111252,-87.8819811,18z/data=!4m13!1m7!3m6!1s0x880fb64f19b2bf39:0x6f505ffb3d0d025!2s1680+E+Touhy+Ave,+Des+Plaines,+IL+60018,+USA!3b1!8m2!3d42.0110613!4d-87.8813635!3m4!1s0x880fb77da91ffa21:0xb6fad06ef8a95916!8m2!3d42.010951!4d-87.8815735)
[Contact Us](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/contact-us)

## Chicago data center overview
### At a glance
  * Phase I expected completion in 2025
  * 15 miles from downtown Chicago
  * Matched by 100% renewable power
  * Chicago metro is the 5th largest data center market in the U.S.


### Campus
  * 13-acre campus
  * Located in Des Plaines
  * 315,000 ft2 of space at CHI-1
  * 8 MW of capacity expected in 2025
  * 36 MW of power at full build
  * Four 28,000+ ft2 data halls
  * Minutes from O’Hare airport


### Ecosystems
  * Carrier-Neutral
  * Cloud-neutral
  * Diverse fiber points of entry
  * Access to local carriers, multiple IXs and major clouds
  * Three redundant MMRs
  * Low latency access to major metros such as Milwaukee, Indianapolis, Detroit, St. Louis and Toronto


### Compliance
  * BREEAM sustainable build targets
  * World-leading compliance program
  * Exceptional design build and operational efficiency

## Our Chicago, Illinois data center & colocation services
##### We provide a full range of certified monitoring, migration and engineering services at all of our facilities worldwide. If you need detailed NOC reporting, a user-friendly customer portal, or full-scale builds and migrations, we can provide a one-off, ongoing or global solution.
  

### Compliance
Trusted by some of the world’s most highly-regulated organizations, Iron Mountain is an industry leader in compliance. Reduce data center risk with our comprehensive compliance support including HIPAA, FISMA High, PCI-DSS, ISO 27001, and SOC 2/3.
### Security
We are the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. Both aboveground and underground, our highly secure data centers have enhanced physical and digital security layers.
### Smart Hands
At every Iron Mountain data center, we offer a full portfolio of remote smart hands services, covering rack and stack services, builds and installs, hardware, power and connectivity as well as general hands-on maintenance tasks. 
### NOC and Portal
Our Global Network Operations Center (GNOC) is your central point for customer communication and advocacy. Leverage our data center portal for ticketing, power & cooling audits, access logs, bandwidth reports and more.
### Network Connectivity
With Iron Mountain’s carrier-neutral networking and data center interconnect services, we’ll get you where you need to be. We offer a wide range of services including cross connects, virtual cross connects, direct internet access, metro waves, peering and internet exchanges as well as Cloud On-Ramp.
### Sustainability
We are firm in our commitment to renewable energy and sustainable data centers. Our facilities are matched by 100% renewable energy, and our customers can take credit for the green energy that Iron Mountain buys on their own sustainability reporting with Green Power Pass.
## Iron Mountain's CHI data center
### Proven track record
Iron Mountain is the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including 90% of the Fortune 1000. The world’s most heavily regulated organizations have trusted us with their data for decades.
###  Global efficiency 
Energize your digital transformation at our Chicago data center via our cloud, network and IT service ecosystems. Enjoy remote data center management, unbeatable operational efficiency and seamless global scale and standards.
###  Hyperscale-ready 
Iron Mountain Data Centers facilities have been designed to scale to accommodate exacting, wholesale requirements of hyperscale cloud providers, government organizations, and global enterprises.
###  Grow as you go 
Rather than relying on legacy infrastructure, your business can deploy data center capacity just like the cloud - as and when you need it. At our Chicago colocation facilities, choose from cabinets, cages, suites, and MODs, and adapt and scale as you go.
> ### Fender customer success story
> #### The challenge
> Fender needed a home for their mission-critical financial planning and e-commerce systems. They looked to maximize redundancy while reducing data center total cost of ownership. Also, Fender needed access to numerous services providers to support their evolving hybrid IT architecture.
> #### The results
> Fender has enjoyed 100% uptime to date and flexible terms that significantly reduced data center costs. They cited Iron Mountain’s certified engineers as the added bonus, relying on Iron Mountain data center services for on-demand needs, extending capabilities and staying focused on high value activities.
> #### In their words
> _“It's one thing to outsource your servers. It’s another to outsource the support for those servers—that’s what gives CIOs heartburn. Iron Mountain’s remote support has been spectacular. Not only do they respond quickly, but they have a team that is well-trained and professional and that gives us confidence that the job will be done right.”_
SVP for Global IT, CIO of Fender

## Why choose our Denver data center (DEN-1)?
DEN-1 is a purpose-built 180,000 ft2 / 14.4 MW colocation facility on a 6-acre campus located just 10 minutes from downtown Denver in one of the lowest-risk US metros for natural disasters.
  1. 6-acre site
  2. 180,000 ft2 of space
  3. 14.4 MW capacity


  

**DEN-1:** [4300 Brighton Blvd. Denver, CO 80216](https://www.google.com/maps/place/Iron+Mountain+Data+Centers+DEN-1/@39.777141,-104.9680842,18z/data=!4m13!1m7!3m6!1s0x876c790961aa1d09:0x93bf409aa43fca24!2s4300+Brighton+Blvd,+Denver,+CO+80216,+USA!3b1!8m2!3d39.7773595!4d-104.968274!3m4!1s0x876c7909616b13a5:0x7b500545dd5ef19f!8m2!3d39.7772483!4d-104.968605)

## Denver data center overview
### At a glance
  * Convenient, secure location near downtown
  * Excellent in-house ecosystems and NSP selection
  * Easy cloud access
  * Low optimal PUE
  * Matched by 100% renewable power


### Campus
  * 6-acre site
  * < 10 minutes from downtown Denver
  * 180,000 ft2 facility
  * Highly efficient operation with market-leading PUE
  * Superior track record for uptime
  * Concurrently maintainable Denver colocation facility
  * 14.4 MW


### Ecosystems
  * 13 network service providers on-site
  * Megaport cloud on-ramp
  * 240+ customer ecosystem
  * WAN connectivity options


### Compliance
  * NIST 800-53
  * FISMA HIGH
  * FedRAMP
  * CMMC
  * SOC 2 Type II, SOC 3 
  * PCI-DSS
  * HIPAA
  * HITRUST
  * ISO 9001, ISO 27001, 50001, 14001, 22301
  * EPA Energy Star

## Our Denver, Colorado data center & colocation services
##### We provide a full range of certified monitoring, migration and engineering services at all of our facilities worldwide. If you need detailed NOC reporting, a user-friendly customer portal, or full-scale builds and migrations, we can provide a one-off, ongoing or global solution.
  

### Compliance
Trusted by some of the world’s most highly-regulated organizations, Iron Mountain is an industry leader in compliance. Reduce data center risk with our comprehensive compliance support including HIPAA, FISMA High, PCI-DSS, ISO 27001, and SOC 2/3.
### Security
We are the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. Both aboveground and underground, our highly secure data centers have enhanced physical and digital security layers.
### Smart Hands
At every Iron Mountain data center, we offer a full portfolio of remote smart hands services, covering rack and stack services, builds and installs, hardware, power and connectivity as well as general hands-on maintenance tasks. 
### NOC and Portal
Our Global Network Operations Center (GNOC) is your central point for customer communication and advocacy. Leverage our data center portal for ticketing, power & cooling audits, access logs, bandwidth reports and more.
### Network Connectivity
With Iron Mountain’s carrier-neutral networking and data center interconnect services, we’ll get you where you need to be. We offer a wide range of services including cross connects, virtual cross connects, direct internet access, metro waves, peering and internet exchanges as well as Cloud On-Ramp.
### Sustainability
We are firm in our commitment to renewable energy and sustainable data centers. Our facilities are matched by 100% renewable energy, and our customers can take credit for the green energy that Iron Mountain buys on their own sustainability reporting with Green Power Pass.
## Iron Mountain's DEN data center
### Proven track record
Iron Mountain is the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. The world’s most heavily regulated organizations have trusted us with their data for decades.
###  Global efficiency 
Energize your digital transformation at our Denver data centers via our cloud, network and IT service ecosystems. Enjoy remote data center management, unbeatable operational efficiency and seamless global scale and standards.
###  Hyperscale-ready 
Iron Mountain Data Centers facilities have been designed to scale to accommodate exacting, wholesale requirements of hyperscale cloud providers, government organizations, and global enterprises.
###  Grow as you go 
Rather than relying on legacy infrastructure, your business can deploy data center capacity just like the cloud - as and when you need it. At our Denver colocation facilities, choose from cabinets, cages, suites, and MODs, and adapt and scale as you go.
> ### Bit Refinery customer success story
> #### The challenge
> BitRefinery - a provider of VMware and Hadoop IaaS nationwide - wanted to expand its Hadoop IaaS offering in the Rocky Mountain region. To do so, it needed to find a Denver colocation facility that was secure, quickly scalable, and capable of keeping its dedicated servers up and running continuously.
> #### The results
> BitRefinery is now able to offer Hadoop hosting and managed services at rates 60-70% cheaper than competitors and has the security, liability and massive capacity to accommodate its current and future colocation requirements.
> #### In their words
> _“Their network, power, and operations are unmatched. They have provided us with the stability, security, and flexibility we need to expand and shape our business.”_
Managing Partner, BitRefinery

# Kansas City data center
Underground colocation facility located 110 feet beneath the Earth’s surface with quick connectivity on-site and additional layers of security.

## Why choose our Kansas City (KCM-1) data center?
Constructed underground, Iron Mountain KCM-1 is a 50,000 ft2 facility with 3.9 MW of power and exceptional reliability and efficiency.
  1. 22-acre site
  2. 50,000 ft2 of space
  3. 3.9 MW capacity


  

**KCM-1:** [6301 Winchester Ave Suite 817 Kansas City, MO 64133](https://www.google.com/maps/place/Iron+Mountain+Data+Centers+KCM-1/@39.0743368,-94.5765006,12z/data=!4m13!1m6!3m5!1s0x87c0e4421b595f4b:0x3b18809ca836084c!2sIron+Mountain+Data+Centers+KCM-1!8m2!3d39.010113!4d-94.5041228!3m5!1s0x87c0e4421b595f4b:0x3b18809ca836084c!8m2!3d39.010113!4d-94.5041228!15sCiVJcm9uIE1vdW50YWluIEthbnNhcyBDaXR5IGRhdGEgY2VudGVyIgOIAQGSARxidXNpbmVzc190b19idXNpbmVzc19zZXJ2aWNl4AEA)

## Kansas City data center overview
### At a glance
  * Underground facility located 110 ft beneath the Earth's surface
  * 50,000 ft2
  * Ultra-reliable and secure
  * Easy cloud and carrier access
  * Low latency
  * Matched by 100% renewable power


### Campus
  * 22-acre site
  * 3.9 MW
  * 10 minutes southeast of downtown Kansas City
  * Nearly unlimited scalability potential
  * Additional layers of security and mitigated disaster risk


### Ecosystems
  * 5 carriers on-site
  * Carrier and cloud neutral facility
  * Diverse regional interconnection points


### Compliance
  * EPA Energy Star
  * NIST 800-53
  * FISMA HIGH
  * FedRAMP
  * CMMC
  * SOC 2 Type II, SOC 3
  * PCI-DSS
  * HIPAA
  * HITRUST
  * ISO 9001, 27001, 50001, 14001, 22301

## Our Kansas City, Missouri data center & colocation services
##### We provide a full range of certified monitoring, migration and engineering services at all of our facilities worldwide. If you need detailed NOC reporting, a user-friendly customer portal, or full-scale builds and migrations, we can provide a one-off, ongoing or global solution.
  

### Compliance
Trusted by some of the world’s most highly-regulated organizations, Iron Mountain is an industry leader in compliance. Reduce data center risk with our comprehensive compliance support including HIPAA, FISMA High, PCI-DSS, ISO 27001, and SOC 2/3.
### Security
We are the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. Both aboveground and underground, our highly secure data centers have enhanced physical and digital security layers.
### Smart Hands
At every Iron Mountain data center, we offer a full portfolio of remote smart hands services, covering rack and stack services, builds and installs, hardware, power and connectivity as well as general hands-on maintenance tasks. 
### NOC and Portal
Our Global Network Operations Center (GNOC) is your central point for customer communication and advocacy. Leverage our data center portal for ticketing, power & cooling audits, access logs, bandwidth reports and more.
### Network Connectivity
With Iron Mountain’s carrier-neutral networking and data center interconnect services, we’ll get you where you need to be. We offer a wide range of services including cross connects, virtual cross connects, direct internet access, metro waves, peering and internet exchanges as well as Cloud On-Ramp.
### Sustainability
We are firm in our commitment to renewable energy and sustainable data centers. Our facilities are matched by 100% renewable energy, and our customers can take credit for the green energy that Iron Mountain buys on their own sustainability reporting with Green Power Pass.
## Iron Mountain's KC data center
### Proven track record
Iron Mountain is the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. The world’s most heavily regulated organizations have trusted us with their data for decades.
###  Global efficiency 
Energize your digital transformation at our Kansas City data centers via our cloud, network and IT service ecosystems. Enjoy remote data center management, unbeatable operational efficiency and seamless global scale and standards.
###  Hyperscale-ready 
Iron Mountain Data Centers facilities have been designed to scale to accommodate exacting, wholesale requirements of hyperscale cloud providers, government organizations, and global enterprises.
###  Grow as you go 
Rather than relying on legacy infrastructure, your business can deploy data center capacity just like the cloud - as and when you need it. At our Kansas City colocation facilities, choose from cabinets, cages, suites, and MODs, and adapt and scale as you go.
> ### Carbonite customer success story
> #### The challenge
> Carbonite needed to find a partner that could provide data resilience, security, compliance, certifications and physical locations that were not susceptible to disasters. The company wanted to get out of the business of managing its own data center and focus on helping their existing customer base.
> #### The results
> Carbonite was able to leverage Iron Mountain’s underground Pennsylvania data center facility for their deployment and focus on the service they provide to their customers rather than worrying about owning and managing their own internal data center.
> #### In their words
> _“The partnership that Carbonite has with Iron Mountain has always been based on trust..They have been focused on our business and that has been very important to us.”_
Senior Director of Operations, Carbonite

## Why choose our Miami data center (MIA-1)?
Located on a 3.4-acre campus in Central North West Miami, our purpose-built MIA-1 data center will be a 150,000 ft2, 16 MW facility and provide exceptional Miami colocation opportunities for ambitious enterprises, cloud & content providers, and large-scale users looking for a long-term high-density solution in South Florida. Our Miami data center will have fiber connections to other Iron Mountain facilities and a strong pipeline of carriers and SDNs. MIA-1 is slated to open in 2026. 
  1. 3.4 acre site
  2. 16 MW expected
  3. 150,000 ft2 of GPU-ready space expected


  

**MIA-1:** [2925 NW 120th Terrace, Miami, Florida, 33167](https://www.google.com/maps/dir//2925+NW+120th+Terrace,+Miami,+FL+33167,+United+States/@25.8852174,-80.2460978,17.75z/data=!4m8!4m7!1m0!1m5!1m1!1s0x88d9b03bc30ca99f:0xb4cfaf1fd5600176!2m2!1d-80.2472065!2d25.8845794?entry=ttu)

## Miami data center overview
### At a glance
  * 150,000 ft2 facility
  * 16 MW of IT capacity
  * GPU-ready high density Miami data center
  * Gateway to Latin America
  * Perfect for enterprises, clouds, content providers and more


### Campus
  * 3.4 acre site in Central North West Miami
  * 26 MVA total power
  * 10 minutes from Miami International Airport
  * AI-Ready


### Ecosystems
  * Redundant MMRs
  * Carrier-neutral
  * Low-latency access to Miami IX hub
  * Fiber connections to other IMDC NA data centers
  * Strong pipeline of carriers/SDNs


### Compliance
  * Matched by 100% renewable power
  * BREEAM build accreditation targeted
  * World-leading compliance program

## Our Miami, Florida data center & colocation services
##### We provide a full range of certified monitoring, migration and engineering services at all of our facilities worldwide. If you need detailed NOC reporting, a user-friendly customer portal, or full-scale builds and migrations, we can provide a one-off, ongoing or global solution.
  

### Compliance
Trusted by some of the world’s most highly-regulated organizations, Iron Mountain is an industry leader in compliance. Reduce data center risk with our comprehensive compliance support including HIPAA, FISMA High, PCI-DSS, ISO 27001, and SOC 2/3.
### Security
We are the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. Both aboveground and underground, our highly secure data centers have enhanced physical and digital security layers.
### Smart Hands
At every Iron Mountain data center, we offer a full portfolio of remote smart hands services, covering rack and stack services, builds and installs, hardware, power and connectivity as well as general hands-on maintenance tasks. 
### NOC and Portal
Our Global Network Operations Center (GNOC) is your central point for customer communication and advocacy. Leverage our data center portal for ticketing, power & cooling audits, access logs, bandwidth reports and more.
### Network Connectivity
With Iron Mountain’s carrier-neutral networking and data center interconnect services, we’ll get you where you need to be. We offer a wide range of services including cross connects, virtual cross connects, direct internet access, metro waves, peering and internet exchanges as well as Cloud On-Ramp.
### Sustainability
We are firm in our commitment to renewable energy and sustainable data centers. Our facilities are matched by 100% renewable energy, and our customers can take credit for the green energy that Iron Mountain buys on their own sustainability reporting with Green Power Pass.
## Iron Mountain's MIA data centers
### Proven track record
Iron Mountain is the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including 90% of the Fortune 1000. The world’s most heavily regulated organizations have trusted us with their data for decades.
###  Global efficiency 
Energize your digital transformation at our Miami data center via our cloud, network and IT service ecosystems. Enjoy remote data center management, unbeatable operational efficiency and seamless global scale and standards.
###  Hyperscale-ready 
Iron Mountain Data Centers facilities have been designed to scale to accommodate exacting, wholesale requirements of hyperscale cloud providers, government organizations, and global enterprises.
###  Grow as you go 
Rather than relying on legacy infrastructure, your business can deploy data center capacity just like the cloud - as and when you need it. At our Miami colocation facility, choose from cabinets, cages, and suites, and adapt and scale as you go.
> ### Fender customer success story
> #### The challenge
> Fender needed a home for their mission-critical financial planning and e-commerce systems. They looked to maximize redundancy while reducing data center total cost of ownership. Also, Fender needed access to numerous services providers to support their evolving hybrid IT architecture.
> #### The results
> Fender has enjoyed 100% uptime to date and flexible terms that significantly reduced data center costs. They cited Iron Mountain’s certified engineers as the added bonus, relying on Iron Mountain data center services for on-demand needs, extending capabilities and staying focused on high value activities.
> #### In their words
> _“It's one thing to outsource your servers. It’s another to outsource the support for those servers—that’s what gives CIOs heartburn. Iron Mountain’s remote support has been spectacular. Not only do they respond quickly, but they have a team that is well-trained and professional and that gives us confidence that the job will be done right.”_
SVP for Global IT, CIO of Fender

## Why choose our Mumbai data centers (MUM-1 & MUM-2)?
MUM-1 is a thriving 50,000 ft2 facility with 2.3 MW of power and a lot of room to grow in the heart of one of the world’s fastest-growing data center markets. The new MUM-2 data center sits on a 120,000 ft2 campus and supports 6 MW of power.
  1. 5.5-acres
  2. 170,000 ft2 of total space at MUM-1 & MUM-2
  3. 8.3 MW of total capacity at MUM-1 & MUM-2


  
MUM-1: [9th Floor, Sigma IT Park, Sector-8, Rabale, Navi Mumbai, 400701 India](https://www.google.com/maps/place/Web+Werks+India+Pvt+Ltd./@19.1411865,73.0086339,20z/data=!4m12!1m6!3m5!1s0x3be7c0a73e7c95f3:0xbfdcffb55161db13!2sSigma+IT+Park!8m2!3d19.1411688!4d73.0087028!3m4!1s0x3be7ceda0bce9ae7:0x60cf30f2082154e9!8m2!3d19.141318!4d73.008839) | **MUM-2:** [R202, Sec-8, Rabale, Navi Mumbai, 400701, India](https://www.google.com/maps/place/R-202,+Sector+8,+MIDC+Industrial+Area,+Rabale,+Navi+Mumbai,+Maharashtra+400701,+India/@19.1413863,73.0087237,20z/data=!4m6!3m5!1s0x3be7c0a70fef5645:0xef33cf0ba3aa0604!8m2!3d19.14143!4d73.008749!16s%2Fg%2F11csfqz5qj?entry=ttu)[Contact Us](https://www.ironmountain.com/data-centers/contact-us)

## Mumbai data centers overview
### At a glance
  * 50,000 ft2, 2.3 MW at MUM-1
  * 120,000 ft2, 6 MW at MUM-2
  * Ultra-efficient and secure
  * Easy cloud and carrier access


### Campus
  * Former Web Werks facility
  * 5.5-acre site in Navi Mumbai
  * Excellent transport links
  * MUM-1 scalable to 4 MW
  * MUM-2 facility next door to MUM-1


### Ecosystems
  * 9 carriers on-site
  * 200+ ISPs
  * DE-CIX, Extreme-IX & NIXI Internet Exchanges
  * Direct cloud access

## Our Mumbai, India data center & colocation services
##### We provide a full range of certified monitoring, migration and engineering services at all of our facilities worldwide. If you need detailed NOC reporting, a user-friendly customer portal, or full-scale builds and migrations, we can provide a one-off, ongoing or global solution.
  

### Compliance
Trusted by some of the world’s most highly-regulated organizations, Iron Mountain is an industry leader in compliance. Reduce data center risk with our comprehensive compliance support including HIPAA, FISMA High, PCI-DSS, ISO 27001, and SOC 2/3.
### Security
We are the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. Both aboveground and underground, our highly secure data centers have enhanced physical and digital security layers.
### Smart Hands
At every Iron Mountain data center, we offer a full portfolio of remote smart hands services, covering rack and stack services, builds and installs, hardware, power and connectivity as well as general hands-on maintenance tasks. 
### NOC and Portal
Our Global Network Operations Center (GNOC) is your central point for customer communication and advocacy. Leverage our data center portal for ticketing, power & cooling audits, access logs, bandwidth reports and more.
### Network Connectivity
With Iron Mountain’s carrier-neutral networking and data center interconnect services, we’ll get you where you need to be. We offer a wide range of services including cross connects, virtual cross connects, direct internet access, metro waves, peering and internet exchanges as well as Cloud On-Ramp.
### Sustainability
We are firm in our commitment to renewable energy and sustainable data centers. Our facilities are matched by 100% renewable energy, and our customers can take credit for the green energy that Iron Mountain buys on their own sustainability reporting with Green Power Pass.
## Iron Mountain's MUM data centers
### Proven track record
Iron Mountain is the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. The world’s most heavily regulated organizations have trusted us with their data for decades.
###  Global efficiency 
Energize your digital transformation at our Mumbai data centers via our cloud, network and IT service ecosystems. Enjoy remote data center management, unbeatable operational efficiency and seamless global scale and standards.
###  Hyperscale-ready 
Iron Mountain Data Centers facilities have been designed to scale to accommodate exacting, wholesale requirements of hyperscale cloud providers, government organizations, and global enterprises.
###  Grow as you go 
Rather than relying on legacy infrastructure, your business can deploy data center capacity just like the cloud - as and when you need it. At our Mumbai colocation facilities, choose from cabinets, cages, suites, and MODs, and adapt and scale as you go.
> ### Krystal customer success story
> #### The challenge
> After fast growth of their own developed cloud solution, Katapult, Krystal realized it needed to scale quickly and spin up an equally responsive and robust global architecture. However, the perfect data center partner had to meet their high ethical and environmental standards.
> #### The results
> Krystal chose Iron Mountain Data Centers for it’s 100% renewable power as well as rooftop solar array (available at select locations). After initially launching in the U.S., the company has since expanded into EMEA and is looking to expand even further into the Asia Pacific region. Katapult is now plugged into the diverse connectivity ecosystems of all Iron Mountain facilities.
> #### In their words
> _“We loved the fact that there was renewable power being generated on-site, but also saw Iron Mountain as a longer-term match due to their standards, their ecosystems and their location spread.”_
Krystal CEO & Founder

## Iron Mountain's New Jersey data center NJE-1
Located in Edison, New Jersey, just 30 miles from NYC and 66 miles from Philadelphia, Iron Mountain's NJE-1 delivers unmatched reliability, security, and connectivity for businesses in the Greater New York region and beyond. This 830,000 square-foot facility, situated on a secure 43-acre campus, features 30 MW of power capacity and multiple infrastructure configurations with concurrently maintainable systems. NJE-1 offers modular data center solutions for rapid deployment and flexible scaling needs.
[Download NJE-1 Brochure](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/files/services/imdc/locations/data-center-new-jersey-brochure.pdf?sc_lang=en)
  * _930k_
Square Feet
  * _30MW_

  * _22+_

  * _18K+_

## Why leading enterprises choose our New Jersey data center (NJE-1)?
![price 1](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/images/brand/icons/grey-background/price-1.svg?h=72&iar=0&w=72&sc_lang=en)
###  Cost Advantage
  
Save significantly with lower taxes and operational expenses. Customers typically save 30-40% compared to New York data centers while maintaining the same level of service and connectivity.​  

![storm](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/images/brand/icons/grey-background/storm.svg?h=72&iar=0&w=72&sc_lang=en)
### Disaster Resilience
  
Flood-resistant location compared to vulnerable Secaucus facilities, providing better disaster resilience for your mission-critical infrastructure.
![Interconnected in the cloud](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/images/brand/icons/grey-background/cloud-interconnected.svg?h=72&iar=0&w=72&sc_lang=en)
### Immediate Scailability
  
Our expansive space allows seamless scaling from single cabinets to dedicated modular data centers without relocating. Deploy additional capacity in weeks, not months.
![brainstorming](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/images/brand/icons/grey-background/brainstorming.svg?h=72&iar=0&w=72&sc_lang=en)
### Excellent Connectivity
  
Excellent connectivity with 22+ carriers, major cloud on-ramps, cross-connects, IP transit, and Metro Wave services.
  

## The advantages of colocation in New Jersey
Lower costs, better resilience, and unlimited growth potential in the heart of the Northeast corridor.
#### Geographic advantages
Easy access to NYC, Philadelphia and the Greater New York Region. Direct highway access via Routes 1 and 287, plus 20 minutes to Newark Liberty International Airport.
#### Regulatory environment
New Jersey's business-friendly tax structure and regulatory environment provide operational budget advantages over urban alternatives. Lower property taxes and competitive utility rates contribute to 30-40% cost savings compared to Manhattan facilities.
#### Market access
Serve customers across the entire Northeast corridor from a single location, including New York, Philadelphia, Boston, Washington D.C., as well as local areas in Edison, Piscataway, New Brunswick, Princeton, Newark, and surrounding Middlesex County communities without the premium costs of multiple urban data center deployments.
[Download Greater New York Market Guide](https://resources.ironmountain.com/whitepapers/d/data-centers-infrastructure-planning-report-north-america-greater-new-york)  

![nje advantages](https://www.ironmountain.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fedge.sitecorecloud.io%2Fironmountain-c8dd68e9%2Fmedia%2Fproject%2Firon-mountain%2Firon-mountain%2Fimages%2Fservices-and-industries%2Fimdc%2Fhero-and-background-over-800px%2Flocations%2Fnje-advantages.png%3Fh%3D911%26iar%3D0%26w%3D850%26sc_lang%3Den&w=1920&q=80)
## New Jersey data center overview![Carrier neutral background](https://edge.sitecorecloud.io/ironmountain-c8dd68e9/media/project/iron-mountain/iron-mountain/images/services-and-industries/imdc/hero-and-background-over-800px/carrier-neutral-colocation-iron-mountain.png?h=550&iar=0&w=1920&sc_lang=en&mw=1920)
  * Size: 830,000 sq ft facility on 43-acre secure campus 
  * Power: 30MW capacity with 2N redundancy 
  * Powered by PSE&G® 
  * Matched by 100% renewable energy 
  * Efficiency: Market-leading PUE with ultra-efficient operations 
  * Cooling: N+1 redundancy with liquid cooling available 
  * Concurrently maintainable systems with TIA-942 certification, ensuring 99.999% uptime
  * 18,000+ rooftop solar panels—the largest installation of any North American data center 
  * Deployment Options: Cabinets, cages, suites, and modular data centers


  * Secure lobby with 24/7 staffing 
  * 24/7/365 Smart Hands 
  * Two-factor access to the facility
  * Three-factor access to the data center floor 
  * Migration Assistance 
  * Iron Mountain Data Centers Customer Portal 
  * Monitored by our Global Network Operations Center (GNOC) 
  * Executive offices and conference rooms 
  * Break areas and collaboration spaces 
  * On-site parking for 500+ vehicles 
  * Industrial-size loading docks with lift gates that can service anything from a small box truck to a 53-foot 18-wheeler


  * Distance to NYC: 30 miles from Manhattan 
  * Location offers superior disaster resilience 
  * Carrier Hotel: 165 Halsey St, Newark, NJ 
  * Highway Access: Routes 1 and 287 
  * Airport: 20 minutes to Newark Liberty International 
  * Service Area: Greater New York Region 
  * Address: [3003 Woodbridge Ave, Edison, NJ 08837](https://www.google.com/maps/place/Iron+Mountain+Data+Centers+NJE-1/@40.5293148,-74.3613278,13z/data=!4m15!1m8!3m7!1s0x89c3c9d07f28da83:0x487d6a686e3abc02!2s3003+Woodbridge+Ave,+Edison,+NJ+08837,+USA!3b1!8m2!3d40.5210834!4d-74.3473835!16s%2Fg%2F11bw3z60gf!3m5!1s0x89c3c9dab1109aa5:0x9202693ba9baed0f!8m2!3d40.5216986!4d-74.3461546!16s%2Fg%2F1tlkd9gm?entry=ttu)


Premium network connectivity without the premium price tag
##### Network Infrastructure:
  * **22+ Carriers:** Direct access to major telecommunications providers
  * **Internet Exchanges:** DE-CIX and IX-Reach on-site for optimized peering
  * **Diverse Entry Points:** Multiple fiber paths ensure redundant connectivity


##### Network Services:
  * **Cross Connects:** High-speed direct connections between customers and carriers
  * **Direct Internet Access & IP Transit:** Multiple Tier 1 provider options for global internet connectivity
  * **Metro Wave:** Dedicated wavelength services for high-bandwidth applications
  * **Cloud On-Ramps:** Direct connections to AWS, Microsoft Azure, Google Cloud
  * **Virtual Cross Connects (Private Network Transport):** Point-to-point L2 connectivity is available between our data centers leveraging Iron Mountain’s network backbone
  * **Software-Defined Networking:** Megaport presence for instant provisioning


Comprehensive certifications meeting the most stringent regulatory and industry standards
##### Global Standards (ISO Certifications):
  * ISO 27001 (Security Management)
  * ISO 50001 (Energy Management)
  * ISO 14001 (Environmental Management)
  * ISO 22301 (Business Continuity)
  * ISO 9001 (Quality Management)


##### Regulated Industries:
  * NIST 800-53, FISMA High, FedRAMP authorized (Government)
  * HIPAA compliant with HITRUST certification (Healthcare)
  * PCI-DSS for payment processing requirements (Financial Services)


##### Infrastructure & Operations:
  * TIA-942 certified infrastructure design
  * SOC 2 Type II and SOC 3 audit reports


##### Environmental & Energy:
  * EPA Energy Star certified for energy efficiency

## Frequently asked questions
What makes Edison, New Jersey, an ideal choice compared to New York data centers?
Edison offers the perfect balance: same world-class connectivity as Manhattan with 30-40% financial savings, a large facility with scalable space, and better disaster resilience. You get NYC-level infrastructure without NYC-level constraints and costs.
What makes Iron Mountain's compliance program different?
We're the only provider with comprehensive global ISO certifications across security, energy, environmental, business continuity, and quality management. This means one partner can meet all your compliance requirements, whether you're in healthcare, financial services, or government.
What sustainability benefits does NJE-1 offer?
NJE-1 operates on 100% renewable energy matching, giving your organization immediate access to clean power. Our Green Power Pass program enables direct sustainability reporting, helping you meet corporate environmental goals and demonstrate measurable progress to stakeholders. The facility, which has a rooftop solar array, meets ISO 14001 environmental management and ISO 50001 energy management standards, ensuring operations align with global sustainability practices.
What makes our New Jersey colocation facility unique?
NJE-1 stands apart with the largest rooftop solar installation of any data center in North America, featuring over 18,000 solar modules that generate 7.2MW of renewable energy power directly on-site. This massive solar array creates an unmatched combination of sustainability, scale and operational efficiency.
What are modular data centers and how quickly can I deploy at NJE-1?
Modular data centers are pre-engineered, self-contained infrastructure units that provide all the power, cooling, and security of a traditional data center in a faster, more flexible deployment model. At NJE-1, our modular solutions allow you to accelerate your infrastructure deployments. Whether you need a few cabinets or multiple modular units, you can scale rapidly without the lengthy build-out timelines of traditional construction. This approach gives you enterprise-grade infrastructure with the agility to respond to changing business demands, all within our secure, compliant facility environment.
What space and power options are available at NJE-1?
NJE-1 offers exceptional flexibility with 830,000 square feet of data center space and 30MW of power capacity with 2N redundancy across 43 acres of land. We provide multiple deployment options to match your specific requirements: individual cabinets for smaller footprints, secure cages for dedicated space, private suites for enhanced control, and full modular data centers for large-scale deployments. Our concurrently maintainable infrastructure means you can start with a single cabinet and seamlessly scale to multi-megawatt deployments without relocating.

## Why choose our Western Pennsylvania data center (WPA-1)?
Iron Mountain’s WPA-1 data center is located 220 feet underground, using a natural cooling lake to optimize energy efficiency and offering unbeatable levels of security and protection.
  1. 315-acre campus located 220 ft. underground
  2. 330,000 ft2 of data center space
  3. 15.5 MW capacity

## Enhanced benefits of Iron Mountain's underground facility in Boyers, PA
Iron Mountain’s underground facility in Boyers, Pennsylvania serves as a highly secure and resilient location for data centers, records management, media archives, and digital transformation services. This 315-acre underground complex is trusted by government agencies, financial institutions, healthcare providers, and major corporations for high-security storage, digital infrastructure, and long-term preservation of sensitive assets.
By leveraging its natural underground environment, the facility offers protection against physical threats, natural disasters, and environmental risks, making it an ideal solution for mission-critical data, classified records, historical documents, valuable media archives, and digital conversion services. 
### Why this matters
For organizations that require maximum security, disaster resilience, digital transformation services, and long-term data preservation, Iron Mountain’s underground facility in Boyers, PA, provides a unique and strategic advantage. The underground environment not only protects assets from external threats but also enables energy-efficient, high-compliance, and sustainable operations—a critical factor in today's risk-conscious and environmentally focused world. 
![Pennsylvania Data Center Cabinet Rows](https://www.ironmountain.com/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fedge.sitecorecloud.io%2Fironmountain-c8dd68e9%2Fmedia%2Fproject%2Firon-mountain%2Firon-mountain%2Fimages%2Fservices-and-industries%2Fimdc%2Fhero-and-background-over-800px%2Fwpa-1-cabinet-row-2.jpg%3Fh%3D480%26iar%3D0%26w%3D856%26sc_lang%3Den&w=1920&q=80)
## Why underground?
Unmatched security & protection
  * Highly Secure Location – Being 220 feet below ground provides a natural layer of security that reduces exposure to external threats, including physical attacks, espionage, and unauthorized access.
  * Limited Entry Points – Access to the facility is tightly controlled with armed checkpoints, biometric authentication, and mantraps, making unauthorized entry extremely difficult.
  * Perimeter Defense & Surveillance – Equipped with CCTV monitoring, metal detectors, and 24/7 security personnel, ensuring constant surveillance and controlled access.


Disaster resilience
  * Protection from Natural Disasters – Unlike traditional above-ground facilities, this underground site is naturally shielded from hurricanes, tornadoes, wildfires, floods, and earthquakes. 
  * Fire & Flood Resistance – The limestone environment is naturally non-flammable and does not require traditional fire suppression systems that could damage sensitive media or data assets. 
  * Temperature & Humidity Stability – The underground setting naturally maintains a stable climate, reducing risks associated with extreme temperature fluctuations and humidity damage.


Digital transformation and digitization capabilities
  * Intelligent Document Processing – The Boyers facility offers advanced digitization services to help organizations transition from physical to digital records, ensuring greater accessibility and efficiency. 
  * Secure Digital Storage & Retrieval – Digitized records can be securely stored and retrieved while maintaining compliance with regulatory requirements. 
  * Supports Long-Term Digital Preservation – Enhances records management strategies by safeguarding valuable historical, government, and corporate documents in digital formats. 


Energy efficiency & sustainability
  * Geothermal Cooling Advantage – The facility benefits from naturally cool underground temperatures, reducing the need for energy-intensive cooling solutions. 
  * Optimal Power Usage Effectiveness (PUE): Due to its stable underground climate and underground aquifer, this natural cooling contributes to higher energy efficiency and low optimal PUE. 
  * Matched by 100% Renewable Power – The facility is 100% matched by renewable energy sources, aligning with modern sustainability goals.


Long-term data & asset preservation
  * Ideal for Media & Archive Storage – The underground setting reduces exposure to environmental pollutants, UV light, and oxidation, preserving delicate materials such as historical records, digital media, film archives, and government documents.
  * Secure Data Center Operations – Mission-critical data storage and backup services benefit from a low-risk, high-resilience environment, ensuring business continuity in case of cyberattacks.


Compliance & regulatory alignment
  * Government-Grade Security & Compliance – The facility is trusted by federal agencies, financial institutions, and healthcare providers, meeting stringent standards such as FedRAMP, NIST 800-53, HIPAA, PCI-DSS, and ISO 27001.
  * FISMA HIGH & FedRAMP-Certified – These certifications demonstrate adherence to the highest levels of data security and operational integrity, making it an attractive choice for government and enterprise customers. 


## Pennsylvania data center overview
### At a glance
  * Extensive ultra-secure underground campus ideal for DR and storage
  * Energy-efficient design using natural lake for cooling
  * Wide selection of carriers
  * 330,000 ft2 of total Iron Mountain Pittsburgh data center space
  * 15.5 MW available power
  * Matched by 100% renewable power
  * Low optimal PUE


### Campus
  * 315-acre underground campus
  * Less than an hour from Pittsburgh
  * Protection against manmade and natural disasters
  * Geothermal lake cooling
  * Nearly unlimited scalability potential
  * Perimeter security, armed checkpoints, metal detectors, mantraps, biometric access, CCTV
  * Concurrently maintainable colocation facility


### Ecosystems
  * Ideal location for hybrid production, backup and storage
  * Wide selection of carriers and cloud access providers
  * Selection of accredited IT service providers
  * Secure cloud backup services on-site
  * Location of preference for secure financial, government and research infrastructure


### Compliance
  * EPA Energy Star
  * TIA-942 facility
  * NIST 800-53
  * FISMA HIGH
  * FedRAMP
  * SOC 2 Type II, SOC 3
  * PCI-DSS
  * HIPAA
  * HITRUST
  * ISO 9001, 27001, 50001, 14001, 22301

## Our Pittsburgh, Pennsylvania data center & colocation services
##### We provide a full range of certified monitoring, migration and engineering services at all of our facilities worldwide. If you need detailed NOC reporting, a user-friendly customer portal, or full-scale builds and migrations, we can provide a one-off, ongoing or global solution.
  

### Compliance
Trusted by some of the world’s most highly-regulated organizations, Iron Mountain is an industry leader in compliance. Reduce data center risk with our comprehensive compliance support including HIPAA, FISMA High, PCI-DSS, ISO 27001, and SOC 2/3.
### Security
We are the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. Both aboveground and underground, our highly secure data centers have enhanced physical and digital security layers.
### Smart Hands
At every Iron Mountain data center, we offer a full portfolio of remote smart hands services, covering rack and stack services, builds and installs, hardware, power and connectivity as well as general hands-on maintenance tasks. 
### NOC and Portal
Our Global Network Operations Center (GNOC) is your central point for customer communication and advocacy. Leverage our data center portal for ticketing, power & cooling audits, access logs, bandwidth reports and more.
### Network Connectivity
With Iron Mountain’s carrier-neutral networking and data center interconnect services, we’ll get you where you need to be. We offer a wide range of services including cross connects, virtual cross connects, direct internet access, metro waves, peering and internet exchanges as well as Cloud On-Ramp.
### Sustainability
We are firm in our commitment to renewable energy and sustainable data centers. Our facilities are matched by 100% renewable energy, and our customers can take credit for the green energy that Iron Mountain buys on their own sustainability reporting with Green Power Pass.
## Iron Mountain's WPA data center
### Proven track record
Iron Mountain is the trusted guardian for more than 230,000 customers including more than 90% of the Fortune 1000. The world’s most heavily regulated organizations have trusted us with their data for decades.
###  Global efficiency 
Energize your digital transformation at our Hyderabad data centers via our cloud, network and IT service ecosystems. Enjoy remote data center management, unbeatable operational efficiency and seamless global scale and standards.
###  Hyperscale-ready 
Iron Mountain Data Centers facilities have been designed to scale to accommodate exacting, wholesale requirements of hyperscale cloud providers, government organizations, and global enterprises.
### Grow as you go 
Rather than relying on legacy infrastructure, your business can deploy data center capacity just like the cloud - as and when you need it. At our Hyderabad colocation facilities, choose from cabinets, cages, suites, and MODs, and adapt and scale as you go.
> ### Carbonite customer success story
> #### The challenge
> Carbonite needed to find a partner that could provide data resilience, security, compliance, certifications and physical locations that were not susceptible to disasters. The company wanted to get out of the business of managing its own data center and focus on helping their existing customer base.
> #### The results
> Carbonite was able to leverage Iron Mountain’s underground Pennsylvania data center facility for their deployment and focus on the service they provide to their customers rather than worrying about owning and managing their own internal data center.
> #### In their words
> _“The partnership that Carbonite has with Iron Mountain has always been based on trust..They have been focused on our business and that has been very important to us.”_
Senior Director of Operations, Carbonite

# Phoenix data centers
Our Phoenix data center campus features North America's first-ever BREEAM design-certified data center (AZP-2) providing sustainable data center design as well as the security, scalability and reduced OPEX that you need.

## Why choose our Phoenix data centers (AZP-1, AZP-2, AZP-3)? 
Just 10 minutes east of downtown Phoenix, Iron Mountain's AZP-1 and AZP-2 data centers offer an unbeatable range of power and interconnection opportunities tailored for enterprises, service providers and hyperscale clouds. A third Phoenix data center, AZP-3, is currently in development.
  1. 39-acre campus
  2. >1,000,000 ft2 of total space on campus
  3. 89 MW total capacity for AZP-1 & AZP-2


  

**AZP-1:** [615 N 48th Street Phoenix, AZ 85008](https://www.google.com/maps/place/Iron+Mountain+Data+Centers+AZP-1/@33.4544312,-111.9757238,17z/data=!4m13!1m7!3m6!1s0x872b0e9882612029:0xecc4e5da86d80385!2s615+N+48th+St,+Phoenix,+AZ+85008,+USA!3b1!8m2!3d33.4544312!4d-111.9757238!3m4!1s0x872b0e98838ef765:0x529def5ea350227b!8m2!3d33.454411!4d-111.976435) | **AZP-2:** [4802 East Van Buren Street Phoenix, AZ 85008](https://www.google.com/maps/place/Iron+Mountain+Data+Centers+AZP-2/@33.4524445,-111.9775635,17z/data=!4m13!1m7!3m6!1s0x872b0e9815548999:0x7f64878e92eb4660!2s4802+E+Van+Buren+St,+Phoenix,+AZ+85008,+USA!3b1!8m2!3d33.4524445!4d-111.9775635!3m4!1s0x872b0f1639f5b9f7:0x98cd172fb2eafe!8m2!3d33.451516!4d-111.9773239)
